  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_1a8f79b0-32b8-40c1-bac2-c1f3de47440f'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);

  <span id="freeText6427486842359169985" style="display:none"><b>They're here. They ride. The Four Horsemen of the Apocalypse.</b><br /><br /><i>Born of a match between good and evil, four siblings stand between hell's minions and everything they want to destroy. They are the <b>Lords of Deliverance</b>, and they have the power to ward off Doomsday...or let it ride...</i><br /><br /><b>LETHAL RIDER</b><br /><br />Thanatos, the most deadly Horseman of the Apocalypse, has endured thousands of years of celibacy to prevent the end of days. But just one night with the wickedly sexy Aegis Guardian, Regan Cooper, shatters centuries of resolve. Yet their passion comes with a price. And Thanatos must face a truth more terrifying than an apocalypse-he's about to become a father.<br /><br />Demon-slayer Regan Cooper never imagined herself the maternal type, but with the fate of the world hanging in the balance she had no choice but to seduce Thanatos and bear his child. Now, as the final battle draws closer and his rage at being betrayed is overshadowed by an undeniable passion for the mother of his child, Thanatos has a life-shattering realization: To save the world, he must sacrifice the only thing he's ever wanted-a family.</span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2959426-mariya?shelf=emotional-wreck">emotional-wreck</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer181474218" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15008168134758486048"><i>
  <b>“Kiss me?” There was a vulnerability in his request that had such a powerful effect on her that she almost choked up. In answer, she lifted her head up and touched her lips to his.</b>
</i><br/><br/><b>LETHAL RIDER</b> was freaking <strong>AMAZING!</strong> It exceeded all of my expectations, but of course, how could Thantos not impress me. This book was full of complete <b>EPIC-NESS!</b> You will be <b>AMAZED</b>. I promise you that! <b>LETHAL RIDER</b> takes place about 8 months after Regan betrayed Thantos into having sex with her to get pregnant. Tha</span>
  <span id="freeText15008168134758486048" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>“Kiss me?” There was a vulnerability in his request that had such a powerful effect on her that she almost choked up. In answer, she lifted her head up and touched her lips to his.</b>
</i><br /><br /><b>LETHAL RIDER</b> was freaking <strong>AMAZING!</strong> It exceeded all of my expectations, but of course, how could Thantos not impress me. This book was full of complete <b>EPIC-NESS!</b> You will be <b>AMAZED</b>. I promise you that! <b>LETHAL RIDER</b> takes place about 8 months after Regan betrayed Thantos into having sex with her to get pregnant. Thantos has been in hell, held and unable to move by the hellhound saliva and does not know that Regan is pregnant. He only has hate for her betrayal and at his siblings for keeping him held down for the past 8 months.<br /><br /><i>
  <b>“I have some more staff members to interrogate.” He winked. “I’ll try to keep their screams at a minimum.” Yeah, he really did have a quirky sense of humor. Especially because she had no doubt he was actually serious.</b>
</i><br /><br />Thantos eventually gets free and comes after Regan only to learn that she is pregnant. He has all kinds of different thoughts and feelings on the subject. Firstly, a baby, a family is all he has ever wanted and he could never have. It seems like a dream come true except that the baby is his agimortus and may possibly be the key to destroying Pestilence. Thantos is determined to keep Regan and the baby safe at all costs.<br /><br /><i>
  <b>"I wasn't lying when I said you’d awakened something sexual in me, something that frankly scares the shit out of me. But that’s my problem, not yours. I won’t make you do anything you don’t want to do.”</b>
</i><br /><br />There were so many moments in the book where I was happy, sad, and angry with rage that it was so funny! Regan betrayed Thantos in the previous book and not only that, but she was going to give the baby to Kynan and Gem to raise thinking she won't be a suitable mother. She has had a rough childhood. But my problem is that even more than halfway through the book almost that she is still talking about giving it to them. She is attached, and this is Thanto's kid too, so he definitely has some say. I mean, the Aegis and her took like everything from him.<br /><br /><i>
  <b>“Here’s how this goes. No Guardians. I don’t trust any of them, including you. You can have as much ice cream as you want. I doubt I’ll stop ordering you around.” He turned his face away and put his lips to her ear. “And you don’t get your own bedroom. You sleep here. With me.</b>
</i><br /><br />I thought Regan had a lot of growing up to do in <b>LETHAL RIDER</b>. I liked her as the heroine, but I felt like she was a bit tortured as well and had a lot of growing to do as a character. Thantos was <b>PERFECTION!</b> We get to learn some interesting things about him and not that we didn't already know this, but <b>HE IS SO FREAKING SEXY! THANTOS IS A GOD!</b> He is definitely my favorite Horseman of the Apocalypse. There were so many moments that I could just rewind and rewind and rewind!<br /><br /><i>
  <b>“So ask me again why I’ll win a battle of wills.” “Fine.” She jammed her feet under the covers. “Why?” “Because I’m immortal and you’re a mere human. I have an eternity to out-stubborn you.”</b>
</i><br /><br />Overall, <b>LETHAL RIDER</b> was <b>JAM-PACKED</b> with nothing but <b>EPIC-NESS!</b> There was so much that happened that I could not possibly explain it all in one single review. I must say this! If you didn't already hate the Aegis, you will want to murder them and wish the most deadliest and most painful death on them! Trust me, you will! I speak the truth! I am really looking forward to Reseph's book and I can already tell from the sneak peek chapter that it is going to be an amazing book.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer8366412868600871767">I had a blast "chatting" with AH about Lethal Rider.... check it out here...<br/><br/><a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://badassbookreviews.com/arc-review-lethal-rider-by-larissa-ione/'>http://badassbookreviews.com/arc-revi...</a><br/><br/><br/><br/>Larissa Ione is by far, one of my favorite authors. In fact, I've not rated any of her books less than 5 stars. When I first rated books, I gave away 5 stars easily, but now- not even close. The fact that all her books still rate so highly just tells you how much I love her as an author. <br/><br/>First, even though you technically don't have to read the Demonica series (the Demonica series </span>
  <span id="freeText8366412868600871767" style="display:none">I had a blast "chatting" with AH about Lethal Rider.... check it out here...<br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://badassbookreviews.com/arc-review-lethal-rider-by-larissa-ione/">http://badassbookreviews.com/arc-revi...</a><br><br><br><br>Larissa Ione is by far, one of my favorite authors. In fact, I've not rated any of her books less than 5 stars. When I first rated books, I gave away 5 stars easily, but now- not even close. The fact that all her books still rate so highly just tells you how much I love her as an author. <br><br>First, even though you technically don't have to read the Demonica series (the Demonica series starts with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/2679633.Pleasure_Unbound__Demonica___1_" title="Pleasure Unbound (Demonica, #1) by Larissa Ione" rel="nofollow noopener">Pleasure Unbound</a> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/2679633.Pleasure_Unbound__Demonica___1_" title="Pleasure Unbound (Demonica, #1) by Larissa Ione" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://s3.amazonaws.com/photo.goodreads.com/books/1289064020s/2679633.jpg" alt="Pleasure Unbound (Demonica, #1) by Larissa Ione" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a>) before reading the Lords of Deliverance series, I really think you should. Some of the characters from the Demonica series show up in Lords of Deliverance series and without reading the Demonica series, you won't quite get the significance of that character.<br><br>Ok, back to Larissa Ione. Not only does Ione tell a story but she manages to continue the story from book to book. She does it without coming across as trying to sell an additional book in her series. It is pretty clear that Ione knows exactly where she is going with the story. However, as a reader, you never feel like the individual book is weak. In fact, everytime Ione finishes a book in her series, I declare it my favorite. OH well. As long as she keeps writing, I'm happy.<br><br>As for this story in this book, I loved the characters. I love the story behind the characters as well. Than can be humorous one minute, and down right scary the next. Regan's insecurities and vulnerability made her duty to her job admirable but at times, I wanted to yell at her. I'm glad she woke up.<br><br>Overall- another 5 star read and my new Ione favorite- until the next one comes out of course.</span>

<div id="review_184036151" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/184036151" />
    <a title="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog"><img alt="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1352609417p2/2489554.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/184036151?book_show_action=true">Jul 11, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" href="/user/show/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog">Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=read-in-2012">read-in-2012</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=warriors">warriors</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=king-of-the-harem">king-of-the-harem</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=my-hottie-harem">my-hottie-harem</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=review-requests">review-requests</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=author-larissa-ione">author-larissa-ione</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=covers-to-covet">covers-to-covet</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer184036151" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10669169204345907216">I have tried to find the perfect word to describe this book. Words such as “dangerously addicting”, “evocative” and “sinful” don’t really encompass all that Larissa Ione has achieved in this series. With dark heroes, spit-fire heroines and an impending doom that threatens to destroy all of mankind, it’s difficult to describe the epic nature of LETHAL RIDER.<br/><br/>Thanatos has been betrayed by The Aegis member, Regan. Rightfully, he wants nothing more from Regan other than her blood on his hands. Howeve</span>
  <span id="freeText10669169204345907216" style="display:none">I have tried to find the perfect word to describe this book. Words such as “dangerously addicting”, “evocative” and “sinful” don’t really encompass all that Larissa Ione has achieved in this series. With dark heroes, spit-fire heroines and an impending doom that threatens to destroy all of mankind, it’s difficult to describe the epic nature of LETHAL RIDER.<br /><br />Thanatos has been betrayed by The Aegis member, Regan. Rightfully, he wants nothing more from Regan other than her blood on his hands. However, when he finds out that Regan is carrying his child, Than takes a step back because he can’t believe that his siblings never informed him about this. For most of this book, Than is angry and violent – just what I love in a hero. As Death, he is merciless so I didn’t expect him to just roll over and comfort Regan after learning about the baby. Than gives Regan a very hard time. He doesn’t accept her apology, however heartfelt they are, because there is a lot more at stake than Regan’s hurt feelings.<br /><br />Ione set up a really difficult challenge for herself. I wondered how she was going to get readers to like Regan again after all that she did to Than. For many, she would not be redeemable. Did I think Ione redeemed Regan by the end of this book? Partly. For the first part of the book, I didn’t think much of Regan. I didn’t hate her, but I also didn’t feel completely attached to her either. However, there is one scene in this book where I think Ione did a fantastic job of evoking sympathy for Regan. When Regan finally breaks down and refuses to have sex with Than because she fears that he will remember the last time they did it, I gained more respect for her. It would have been so easy to allow them to just get on with the hot and heavy sex scene, but the fact that Ione chose to pause there and insert that vulnerable scene made me see Regan in a whole different light. Somehow, I didn’t think Regan was so bad after all.<br /><br />There are many familiar faces in this book. Everyone comes back in one way or the other and it’s nice to see the way the demons from the Demonica series integrate with Horsemen. I have to admit that I’m partial to Wraith. He seems to have the best scenes. <br /><br />Speaking of scenes, there were many high points on this book. Ione doesn’t pull her punches and this book had me blinking several times because I just couldn’t believe what I was reading. It is clear that Ione has planned out her series carefully because every little detail seems to match up perfectly. There were some times when I felt that some scenes were too rushed. I would have loved to have the chance to slow down a few particular scenes just so we could get more of the character’s POV. <br /><br />Thanks to Ione’s great imagination, readers are guaranteed to love this latest chapter in the Lords of Deliverance series. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="10669169204345907216" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer308769609" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11697667642932136726">This series just keeps getting better and better!!!<br/><br/>Lethal Rider, the 3rd book in the Lords of Deliverance Series, begins 8 months after book 2, where the sh…..t hit the fan after Thanatos discovers the truth about Regan Cooper, a demon-slayer working for the Aegis real intentions after they had spent a night of wicked passion and giving her something unique of his…. <br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439216110i/15809442.jpg' alt=' photo hhd-108b_zps1c4e05b0.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>After escaping from his sedated state, he’s out for blood….and vengeance…Regan being his target. <blockquote><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439216110i/15809443.jpg' alt=' photo Demonica-by-Larissa-Ione_zps2phblwdj.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/></blockquote> And hello…not only betrayal but h</span>
  <span id="freeText11697667642932136726" style="display:none">This series just keeps getting better and better!!!<br><br>Lethal Rider, the 3rd book in the Lords of Deliverance Series, begins 8 months after book 2, where the sh…..t hit the fan after Thanatos discovers the truth about Regan Cooper, a demon-slayer working for the Aegis real intentions after they had spent a night of wicked passion and giving her something unique of his…. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439216110i/15809442.jpg" alt=" photo hhd-108b_zps1c4e05b0.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>After escaping from his sedated state, he’s out for blood….and vengeance…Regan being his target. <blockquote><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439216110i/15809443.jpg" alt=" photo Demonica-by-Larissa-Ione_zps2phblwdj.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></blockquote> And hello…not only betrayal but he discovers that Regan is pregnant with his child….just what he needed…a child was, he believed, the only thing that could break his seal. He’s on the warpath and he will make her suffer the same way he did…Angry…fuming…he’s beyond livid… <blockquote><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439216110i/15809444.png" alt=" photo 40d48af4-3f4f-440e-90cf-eec1e9d87120_zpsqdsa3gso.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></blockquote> And what happens when he kidnaps her and spirits her away to his hiding place???? <br><br>That his flipping brother Reseph aka Pestilence had drugged him and Regan on their night of passion so she could get pregnant and break Thanatos’s seal….talk about little devious demon???? The revelation of this betrayal has made him realize that he has to do everything to keep Regan and his child safe and away from Pestilence.<br><br>From enemies to lovers!!!! <br><br>Regan wanting to make things right with Thanatos…..<blockquote><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439216110i/15809445.jpg" alt=" photo 3d3f586bf626c43cd94cfeadd5aae7e5_zpshzsfsm6v.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></blockquote><br>Thanatos realizes how much he wants Regan in his life. <blockquote><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439216110i/15809446.jpg" alt=" photo 0cbb4bafeb46e3c25facbb142b9de51d_zpsbcjewyuj.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></blockquote> How much he wants his own family. <br>The longing, the sexual tension, the chemistry, wanting to share their feelings for each other…..<blockquote><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439216110i/15809447.jpg" alt=" photo images_zpsud2jvj5o.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></blockquote> All the drama and all that happens around this couple is totally unbelievable…everyone out there wants something from them…and that is the child Regan is carrying.<br><br>This is a beyond twisted family…treachery from all sides…..evil forces at play – what sacrifices will you have to make to save the world from destruction??<br><br>The series of events leading to the most unexpected and shocking conclusion…left me thinking…. What??? No, can that ever be possible???<blockquote><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439216110i/15809448.jpg" alt=" photo 4723473_f520_zpshizvg7ff.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></blockquote> I cannot wait!!!!!<br>We are going to be in for a huge surprise…..a shocking revelation of “earthquake” proportions!!!!! <span id="freeTextContainer15868447803257664341"><b>Thanatos</b> i.e. meaning Death in Greek language<br/><br/>He used to be a nice, cool guy. He was the father of all vampires. He loved his brothers and sister, his lovely home and his isolation. <br/>He had to save the world of course, not to let his seal be broken and stop his half-lunatic brother from killing every living thing on the face of Earth from plagues.<br/>But he was also one of the four Horsemen, proud and strong, dark and dangerous, high and mighty.<br/><br/>“Lethal Rider” starts with him drugged and powerless for </span>
  <span id="freeText15868447803257664341" style="display:none"><b>Thanatos</b> i.e. meaning Death in Greek language<br /><br />He used to be a nice, cool guy. He was the father of all vampires. He loved his brothers and sister, his lovely home and his isolation. <br />He had to save the world of course, not to let his seal be broken and stop his half-lunatic brother from killing every living thing on the face of Earth from plagues.<br />But he was also one of the four Horsemen, proud and strong, dark and dangerous, high and mighty.<br /><br />“Lethal Rider” starts with him drugged and powerless for almost 9 months by his brother and sister who were scared that he will snap at any moment. His precious virginity was stolen by a devious Aegis agent in the end of “Immortal Rider”. Thanatos stays immobilized. He is seeing red, he is burning inside and he is planning death for the tortuous, manipulative, rapist Regan. <br />Okay, he is really really angry and scary.<br /><br />The good thing is that obviously his seal is not broken yet, although everyone thought that it was connected with his virginity.<br /><br />Regan. Poor, scared to death (literally), victim of the circumstances, very much pregnant girl. There will be no hole to hide when Thanatos (the future father) gets his powers back! <br /><br />The book is their lovestory and it is full of revenge, a very slow process of forgiveness and large quantities of passion and love.<br /><br />My favorite book from the Lords of Deliverance series!</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer1511294661034257260">I REALLY enjoyed the sizzling chemistry between Thanados and Reagan in this one. Thanados was tricked into having sex with Reagan in the previous book, and where we’re introduced in this one, she’s nine months pregnant with his child. She was sent in as a spy to try to conceive the child of this particular horseman, as there was a prophecy that the child could stop the Apocalypse from coming, so, not cool from his pov, but kind of understandable, too.   <span id="freeText1511294661034257260" style="display:none">I REALLY enjoyed the sizzling chemistry between Thanados and Reagan in this one. Thanados was tricked into having sex with Reagan in the previous book, and where we’re introduced in this one, she’s nine months pregnant with his child. She was sent in as a spy to try to conceive the child of this particular horseman, as there was a prophecy that the child could stop the Apocalypse from coming, so, not cool from his pov, but kind of understandable, too. Who wants the world to end? They are reunited just before she’s due to give birth, and the anger/unresolved feelings there are quite steaming. <br /><br />I enjoyed as well the conflict between the siblings as they try to decide what to do about fallen brother Ressup (Pestilence) who has been causing trouble for three books now and is unleashing plagues all over the planet. Thanados has one of the most conflicted reactions of the three horsemen we’ve seen, and that was interesting to read. My favorite of the series so far! <br /><br />Please excuse typos/name misspellings. Entered on screen reader.<br /></span>

    <a title="Kayla" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7710998-kayla"><img alt="Kayla" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1499808186p2/7710998.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/322641242?book_show_action=true">May 02, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kayla" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kayla" href="/user/show/7710998-kayla">Kayla</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer322641242" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16481095395712702359">OMFG! Where to start, where to start? Larissa has reminded me why I love to read in the first place, I literally devoured this book in a day... Yeah, it was that good! It captured me and sucked me in so I couldn't put it down until I was finished. I'm so serious, I was reading this while I was at my Internship.<br/><br/>The story picks up with Regan being protected in the Aegis headquarters and that's when things get all wound up, Thanatos finds out where Regan is and I'm not going to tell you what happen</span>
  <span id="freeText16481095395712702359" style="display:none">OMFG! Where to start, where to start? Larissa has reminded me why I love to read in the first place, I literally devoured this book in a day... Yeah, it was that good! It captured me and sucked me in so I couldn't put it down until I was finished. I'm so serious, I was reading this while I was at my Internship.<br /><br />The story picks up with Regan being protected in the Aegis headquarters and that's when things get all wound up, Thanatos finds out where Regan is and I'm not going to tell you what happens from there. I know there was a lot of mixed feelings about the scene in Immortal Rider with Regan and Than... you guys know what I'm talking about. Well when I read it I was baffled at first because I considered it rape... but trust and believe me on this one Larissa knew what she was doing! I wish I would have trusted her to begin with, and I will never doubt her again. I am so glad that she took the risk she did because it put a lot of pieces together in Lethal Rider. You really get to see who Regan truly is and that is a selfless, brave, fighter! With that being said let me get back to why I enjoyed Lethal Rider oh so much.<br /><br />Thanatos and Regan's relationship is the MAIN reason... it didn't happen all at once, and they didn't commit themselves to a relationship at first. They both really got to know each other, and see sides of each other that other people have never seen. Their relationship was amazing! Than and Regan's sexual tension had me burning up like a 800 degree oven... that's how hot it was. There are a lot of great things revealed in this book that I will let you discover on your own because it makes the book so enjoyable. I had a lot of OMG, really moments. I am so glad that Thanatos finally gets his heart's desire... a child. While the relationship was awesome, what was even more awesome is Regan and Thanatos's love and sacrifice for their baby. Their baby is what really brought them so close together.<br /><br />This was a kick ass, burning hot, and adventurous book. This is definitely 2012 release you DO NOT want to miss, I loved every second of it and can't get it out of my head after reading it. The sneak peak for Rogue Rider killed/teased me so bad! Can't wait to get my hands on the fourth book... I can't wait to see what the lovely Larissa has in store for Reseph!</span>
  <a data-text-id="16481095395712702359" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_310059472" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/310059472" />
    <a title="Tasha" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6485684-tasha"><img alt="Tasha" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1333763341p2/6485684.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/310059472?book_show_action=true">Apr 10, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tasha" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tasha" href="/user/show/6485684-tasha">Tasha</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/13015843-lethal-rider">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6485684-tasha?shelf=not-sure-how-i-feel-about-this">not-sure-how-i-feel-about-this</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6485684-tasha?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6485684-tasha?shelf=heroines-i-can-t-stand">heroines-i-can-t-stand</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6485684-tasha?shelf=2-stars">2-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6485684-tasha?shelf=whatevs">whatevs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6485684-tasha?shelf=girl-bye">girl-bye</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6485684-tasha?shelf=demons">demons</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer310059472" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1191290527242367840">*takes off my invisible reading glasses and pinches the bridge of my nose*<br/><br/>And the fuckery continues, it appears.<br/><br/>I'm not even going to bother doing a summary of this, this...<i>thing</i> because I have a feeling that it would just infuriate me more. As we know from the previous installment, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8843801.Eternal_Rider__Lords_of_Deliverance___1_' title='Eternal Rider (Lords of Deliverance, #1) by Larissa Ione' rel='nofollow noopener'>Eternal Rider</a>, we get to follow Regan <s>the Rapist</s> and Thanatos AKA the Death Horsemen. Let me just get to the point. I'm not quite sure what the hell to think. On some levels, I liked it. Kind of. On most other levels</span>
  <span id="freeText1191290527242367840" style="display:none">*takes off my invisible reading glasses and pinches the bridge of my nose*<br /><br />And the fuckery continues, it appears.<br /><br />I'm not even going to bother doing a summary of this, this...<i>thing</i> because I have a feeling that it would just infuriate me more. As we know from the previous installment, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8843801.Eternal_Rider__Lords_of_Deliverance___1_" title="Eternal Rider (Lords of Deliverance, #1) by Larissa Ione" rel="nofollow noopener">Eternal Rider</a>, we get to follow Regan <s>the Rapist</s> and Thanatos AKA the Death Horsemen. Let me just get to the point. I'm not quite sure what the hell to think. On some levels, I liked it. Kind of. On most other levels, I once again wanted to throw my Kindle at wall (again). Though, I can gladly report, I had less throwing urges than I did last time around.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>What I Liked:</i>
</b><br /><br /><b>Pestilence</b>: I've never come across a villain that I liked so much. Reseph/Pestilence/what-the-fuck-ever is just deliciously evil. For the past 3 books, he has been absolutely wiping the floor with #teamgood and I loved it. Though I must wonder if I genuinely liked him that much or did I hate everyone else so much more that he just automatically became appealing.<br /><br /><b>Thanatos during the first 40% of the book</b>: I liked Than during the beginning of the book. I liked that he was pissed at Regan. Granted, some of the things he said was ruthlessly harsh BUT I can't say that I fault him for it. The guy was taken advantage of for crying out loud. And as soon as he starting to become my favorite, he went and became stupid. Idiot.<br /><br /><b>Wraith:</b> I like him. I like seeing him. End.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>What I HATED:</i>
</b> (Prepare yourself, this is a biggie.)<br /><br /><b>Kynan and the Aegis:</b> I am absolutely, positively sick and tired of the jackassery that is this organization. They're stupid and dumb and I am quite shocked that were around for those alleged thousands of years that they claimed they existed. And Kynan, Mr. Part-time Angel, Full-time leader of the Jackassery, sir, I would like to personally punch you in the face. <br /><blockquote>I didn't realize how deep some of our members' resentment of you went, or I'd have stepped in, and I'll never forgive myself for not paying better attention.</blockquote><br />If this isn't the biggest crock of shit I've ever heard. You're telling me in the god knows how many years Regan has been there, you didn't notice that everyone was being an asshole to her? That everyone was just ragging on her for fun? That she was treated like a piece of shit? Sir, please direct yourself to the nearest seat and park your ass in it. Thanks, Management.<br /><br /><b>Regan:</b> I hate this wench. She's a rapist and there is absolutely no way to get around it. The fact that they (Regan and Thanatos) blame this on the drugged wine or whatever the hell they drank is disgusting to say the least. She knew EXACTLY what she was doing; she knew what her intentions were for being there; she heard him say NO. And yet, she kept on riding like a jockey in the Kentucky Derby. Nasty wench. And I absolutely cannot believe that Ms. Ione pulled the sympathy card with her. "Oh poor me, my daddy was possessed and knocked up my mom who then gave me away. Nobody wanted me." Blah, blah, blah, boo freaking hoo. Cry about it in therapy; I have no sympathy for you, Rapey.<br /><br /><b>Thanatos in the Second half:</b> My god, he became such a sap. I don't understand how the hell he was raging mad one minute, then madly in love with Rapey the next. I can understand that you would want to be cordial with the mother of your kid but she violated you, dude! Idk about you but there is no way in hell, I would want to be with a person that took advantage of me. But then again, this is PNR. *rolls eyes dramatically*<br /><br /><b>Gethel:</b> Somebody come get this bitch! Really?! Really?! Like seriously, really?! You set ALL of that in motion because the Horsemen didn't give 2 fucks and a donkey about you not being their Watcher anymore. Girl, bye!<br /><br /><b>The Ending:</b> This was one of those blink and you miss it kind of endings. It was wayyyy too anti-climatic for me. With all the shit that Pestilence has been doing for however long he was running around, he dies like that? Talk about going out with a whimper.<br /><br />Now considering all the foolery, fuckery and jackassery that took place up and down this book, I think I should give this 2 stars. Let's see how I feel in the next couple of days.<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="1191290527242367840" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_332710378" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/332710378" />
    <a title="Jen Davis" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4669344-jen-davis"><img alt="Jen Davis" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1548427639p2/4669344.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/332710378?book_show_action=true">May 19, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jen Davis" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jen Davis" href="/user/show/4669344-jen-davis">Jen Davis</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Mass Market Paperback 9780446574501" href="/book/show/13057150-lethal-rider">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer332710378" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15103333389468378729">Without a doubt, this is the best installment in the Lords of Deliverance series so far. Ever since she introduced us to the Demonica world back in <i>Pleasure Unbound</i>, Larissa Ione has seamlessly woven all of these amazing characters and threads of storylines together into a giant ongoing masterpiece of action, betrayal, romance, epic world-building, and mind-blowing sex. Each book builds on the last. Each leaves me excited, satisfied, and still wanting more.<br/><br/>It's been eight months since the events</span>
  <span id="freeText15103333389468378729" style="display:none">Without a doubt, this is the best installment in the Lords of Deliverance series so far. Ever since she introduced us to the Demonica world back in <i>Pleasure Unbound</i>, Larissa Ione has seamlessly woven all of these amazing characters and threads of storylines together into a giant ongoing masterpiece of action, betrayal, romance, epic world-building, and mind-blowing sex. Each book builds on the last. Each leaves me excited, satisfied, and still wanting more.<br /><br />It's been eight months since the events of <i>Immortal Rider</i>, and Regan is just a couple of weeks away from delivering her baby. Thanatos has been drugged and immobilized all this time. But suddenly, he is able to overcome the drugs and make his way to her. He is drawn to his child, though he has no idea that is the case until he comes face to face with Regan. He is enraged and yet still attracted to the woman who took his virginity. Unsure of where his feelings for her will land, he kidnaps her from an Aegis stronghold and brings her back to his home.<br /><br />Regan struggles to convince Thanatos that she never intended to rape him. That she was drugged. That she was trying to save the world. But his forgiveness is slow in coming. The story follows the two of them as they try to sort out their feelings for one another and protect their unborn child from Pestilence, who knows that destroying the baby with break his brother's seal.<br /><br />Both Thanatos and Regan have some serious issues to overcome. But I really enjoyed their journey. Regan has never had a place she truly belonged and it's gratifying to see her finding a home with the new family she is creating. Thanatos has some major secrets and he's a very dangerous guy. (He is Death after all.) But he is such a softie underneath it all. All he wants in life is a family. Well, that and to get laid. Ione has got some serious skills to make pregnancy sex sexy. Having been nine-months pregnant twice, myself, I can tell you that is no small feat. Yet she does it, so big, big props for that.<br /><br />I love that we're still seeing old familiar characters like Eidolon and the UG folks, front and center in the book. Not only are we getting updates on their lives, but they are part of the ongoing plot. In addition, there are major developments in the Demonica world, from an overhaul of the Aegis --to Pestilence and the overall horsemen arc-- to dire straits for our friend Reaver. Oh Reaver, I love you so. As much as I am looking forward to Reseph's book, it's Reaver's story I am dying for. Reaver and... Harvester? Anyone with me?<br /><br />I loved it.<br /><br />Rating: A<br /><br /><i>*ARC Provided by NetGalley</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="15103333389468378729" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_200504110" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/200504110" />
    <a title="Pamela / SpazP" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3522886-pamela-spazp"><img alt="Pamela / SpazP" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1413901548p2/3522886.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/200504110?book_show_action=true">Aug 20, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Pamela / SpazP" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Pamela / SpazP" href="/user/show/3522886-pamela-spazp">Pamela / SpazP</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/13015843-lethal-rider">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer200504110" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2296009391763180360">(spoiler free)<br/>Larissa Ione is back with her third Lords of Deliverance novel, Lethal Rider, and it's totally worth the wait!<br/><br/>Thanatos has been kept immobile for the past 8 months by his own siblings, Ares and Limos. Upon discovering Regan's horrible deception in Immortal Rider, he went nuclear and squashed a lot of lives. They feel it's for his own good and only intend to keep him in that state until his baby is born. Hades has his own agenda, and helps break him out of his hellhound saliva-induc</span>
  <span id="freeText2296009391763180360" style="display:none">(spoiler free)<br />Larissa Ione is back with her third Lords of Deliverance novel, Lethal Rider, and it's totally worth the wait!<br /><br />Thanatos has been kept immobile for the past 8 months by his own siblings, Ares and Limos. Upon discovering Regan's horrible deception in Immortal Rider, he went nuclear and squashed a lot of lives. They feel it's for his own good and only intend to keep him in that state until his baby is born. Hades has his own agenda, and helps break him out of his hellhound saliva-induced paralysis. Naturally, he immediately goes and finds Regan where she is hiding at The Aegis headquarters. We learn that Regan has been living the past 8 months in shame and fear over what she did to Thanatos. She knew she should not have run, yet she did, and is living with the sickening dreams of the guilt she feels. She is not surprised when he shows up for her.<br /><br />I really wanted to hate Regan, I mean I had a huge hate-on for her at the end of the previous book for what she did to Than. I did not understand how she could do what she did. The beauty of Lethal Rider is that we see Regan's point of view 8 months later with hindsight, and we see just how tortured she is over what she did. We know what motivated her, and we get her backstory that helped to explain what drove her. I don't even feel like I had to work to like Regan, really, and I don't remember even when it happened. I felt like I could understand more of what she did and why she did it and after a while I just didn't care what she did. I wanted her and Than to be together and to have their little "pony boy" together. I felt like they both deserved to be a family, so badly. If folks are worried that she is unredeemable, their worries will be laid to rest. Than gives her soooo muuuuch shiiiiiit, that you really begin to empathize with her. You heart aches, and once they finally allow themselves to try to think ahead and move forward, you are cheering them on.<br /><br />"No matter how bad Kynan's news is, I've got you, okay?" - Thanatos<br /><br />With the events going on with the two of them, there is also Pestilence raping and pillaging the world, and also trying to maneuver other fractions against his brothers ands sister. We get some flashbacks of how he was was Reseph, and the ache it must feel to watch what he has become once his Seal has broken. There is no question for me, thanks to a discussion with Bookaholic Cat, that Reaver is somehow involved in the Horsemen's parentage, mostly because he cannot remember his life prior to falling. Larissa Ione mentions very often throughout this book in particular that the Horsemen are part angel, and one big daddy-contender in Lethal Rider is ruled out. The Fallen Angel drama that goes on between Reaver, Harvester and Gethal is very good, and definitely adds to the overall story. Also, major things happen with The Aegis! Betrayal, and really good action stuff, and I love the direction she has taken things in with that. If you've been missing those Seminus demon brothers, have no fear, they get plenty of scenes! We get to see Eidolon and Shade and Wraith, and their lines are memorable as always.<br /><br />The set up for the 4th book, Rogue Rider, is made for Reseph/Pestilence. I'm a little nervous how that is going to play out, but I was just as equally nervous with how Thanatos's story would play out too, and I loved it. If anyone can redeem a character, it is Larissa Freaking Ione.<br /><br />All of the elements I expect from Larissa Ione are here. Gore, great mythology, action, and hot steamy smexy times. This was probably the easiest book of the three, so far, to follow just because most of the world-building has been laid out previously. I remember really struggling initially with the first book, even though I'd read the Demonica series, because the world building was so dense. That's not a complaint at all, but it's worth remarking on just how seamlessly everything flowed in Lethal Rider. I assumed that there would only be 4 books in this series since there are 4 Horsemen, but goodreads shows there are 5 books slated, so... YAY! MOAR LoD!! In summary, fans of this series will not be disappointed!<br /><br /><a href="http://wp.me/puDkz-5xT" rel="nofollow noopener">Originally posted at WickedLilPixie Reviews</a></span>

<div id="review_246117530" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/246117530" />
    <a title="AH" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3255548-ah"><img alt="AH" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1275413869p2/3255548.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/246117530?book_show_action=true">Dec 12, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="AH" class="user" itemprop="url" name="AH" href="/user/show/3255548-ah">AH</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Mass Market Paperback 9780446574501" href="/book/show/13057150-lethal-rider">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3255548-ah?shelf=angels">angels</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3255548-ah?shelf=demons">demons</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3255548-ah?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3255548-ah?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3255548-ah?shelf=babr-reviews">babr-reviews</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3255548-ah?shelf=zzread-apr-2012">zzread-apr-2012</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3255548-ah?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3255548-ah?shelf=arc-netgalley">arc-netgalley</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3255548-ah?shelf=alpha-males">alpha-males</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer246117530" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13401835414800657037">Thanatos is mad as hell…and he wants to stomp around and shout a bit…<br/><br/><b>Lethal Rider</b> is the third book of Larissa Ione’s <i>Lords of Deliverance</i> series. This series expands upon her earlier <i>Demonica</i> series. The author creates a rich, textured world, full of angels, demons, vampires, and the like. This world is on the cusp of an apocalypse of Biblical proportions brought about by one of the Four Horsemen of the Apocalypse – Pestilence.<br/>In each of her Lord of Deliverance books, the author focused on one </span>
  <span id="freeText13401835414800657037" style="display:none">Thanatos is mad as hell…and he wants to stomp around and shout a bit…<br /><br /><b>Lethal Rider</b> is the third book of Larissa Ione’s <i>Lords of Deliverance</i> series. This series expands upon her earlier <i>Demonica</i> series. The author creates a rich, textured world, full of angels, demons, vampires, and the like. This world is on the cusp of an apocalypse of Biblical proportions brought about by one of the Four Horsemen of the Apocalypse – Pestilence.<br />In each of her Lord of Deliverance books, the author focused on one of the Four Horsemen of the Apocalypse. Eternal Rider focused on Ares or War. The second book Immortal Rider was Limos’ or Famine’s story. This book is Thanatos’ or Death’s story. <br /> <br />Mild spoilers for the previous book may occur in this review – I’ll try to avoid them as much as possible.<br /><br />When we last left Thanatos in Immortal Rider, he had been, shall we say, compromised. In order to stave off the inevitable, his brother and sister Ares and Limos put Than in an induced paralysis. Our story begins as Than wakes from his paralysis. He’s mad as hell, and he wants revenge. <br /><br />The source of Than’s troubles Regan, has some problems of her own and they all seem to rest on her “…little pony.” I didn’t really like Regan in the previous book. In this book, she shines. First of all, she is flawed – she suffers from OCD so much so that she rearranges all of Thanatos’ stuff. She is also not fully human, which gives her some unique sensitivities. Regan has a lot of issues to sort through and I liked how her character developed throughout the story.<br /> <br />Whenever Thanatos was in a scene, I kept envisioning a kind of tattooed caveman stomping around and beating upon his chest. He’s mad at his family. He’s mad at Regan. He wants justice and a choice. One of my favorite scenes was a flashback of Thanatos and Reseph talking before Reseph’s seal broke. They were talking about having a normal life and family. When Reseph asks Thanatos if he would have a mate and family, Thanatos replies:<blockquote>“In a heartbeat,”…”I would give up everything, my very soul, to have just one human lifetime with a mate and children.”</blockquote><br />Thanatos’ character surprised me and I liked what I saw.<br /><br />There is no “insta-love” between Regan and Thanatos. Both characters are at odds with each other. Yet, when another male looks at Regan, Than has some alpha-male issues. He even slipped up and called her mate!<br /><br />Meanwhile, there is a lot of political maneuvering within the Aegis and the angel hierarchy. There are a few surprising betrayals – never saw those coming! There are also a few unexpected alliances. One revelation near the end left me astonished.<br /> <br />With regards to our favorite bad guy Pestilence/Reseph, I don’t know, this destruction of the world stuff began to grow old. Just how much death, destruction, and mayhem could a Horseman of the Apocalypse bring about? <br /><br />I really enjoyed the cameo appearances of the Demonica characters in this book. Eidolon, Shade, Wraith, Con, and Kynan appear in this book. I missed that sexy seminal demon doctor Eidolon.<br /> <br />Larissa Ione is a master storyteller. <b>Lethal Rider</b> is an incredibly exciting read. I could not put the book down. I can’t wait to read the next book in the series – Reseph’s story – Rogue Rider. December 2012 seems so far away!<br /><br /><b>Update - May 31, 2012 - Michelle and I discuss the book on <a href="http://badassbookreviews.com/arc-review-lethal-rider-by-larissa-ione/" rel="nofollow noopener">Badass Book Reviews</a></b>.<br /><br /><i>Thank you to NetGalley and Grand Central Publishing for a review copy of this book.</i><br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="13401835414800657037" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_194597698" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="♡Karlyn P♡" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1131400-karlyn-p"><img alt="♡Karlyn P♡" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1389996373p2/1131400.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/194597698?book_show_action=true">Aug 04, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="♡Karlyn P♡" class="user" itemprop="url" name="♡Karlyn P♡" href="/user/show/1131400-karlyn-p">♡Karlyn P♡</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1131400-karlyn-p?shelf=audiobook">audiobook</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1131400-karlyn-p?shelf=genre-paranromal">genre-paranromal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1131400-karlyn-p?shelf=read-2012">read-2012</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1131400-karlyn-p?shelf=published-2012">published-2012</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer194597698" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16512928444489381261">Wonderful story, but I might be done with this series.<br/><br/>This was Thanatos and Regan's story. He is one of the Four Horsemen of the Apocalypse, and she a human Aegis Guardian. After tricking Thanatos into having sex with her (in book 2), she is now pregnant with a son who could either start or end the apocalypse. <br/><br/>I couldn't wait for their story, and it paid off. I loved both of these two, and the twist with having their unborn son be such a prominent character worked great. BUT... despite loving th</span>
  <span id="freeText16512928444489381261" style="display:none">Wonderful story, but I might be done with this series.<br /><br />This was Thanatos and Regan's story. He is one of the Four Horsemen of the Apocalypse, and she a human Aegis Guardian. After tricking Thanatos into having sex with her (in book 2), she is now pregnant with a son who could either start or end the apocalypse. <br /><br />I couldn't wait for their story, and it paid off. I loved both of these two, and the twist with having their unborn son be such a prominent character worked great. BUT... despite loving this book, I don't think I'll read the next. Not sure, but I think I'm done. <br /><br />Why? I really did love this book, but this series might be getting TOO complex for me! There are soooooo many moving parts to this series - and soooooo much to follow, remember, and understand. There are story arcs from previous books in this series, plus characters and locations that were introduced in a completely different series. So much magic and other PNR rules/twists to remember. <br /><br />Glossary or not, I finally had to let some of the world building fly over my head and just focus on the romance aspect. I am glad I read a few books in the Demonica series, as it helped me understand this complicated story, but I'll admit to being lost quite a bit while reading this book. I can't imagine anyone reading this book as a stand-alone, it would be a monumental struggle to follow along. <br /><br />I wish I would have waited until all books are out, than I could read them closer together and not struggle so much. I feel like I need a PhD in Demonica world-building in order to fully process this one. Frankly, I found that killing my enjoyment of this series. Despite enjoying this series thus far, I don't think I can take on yet another layer of even more world-building rules, characters, consequences, and story arcs. <br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="16512928444489381261" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText7149621768565071174" style="display:none">*spoilers alert!*<br><br>I have strict reservations when posting (hard core) profanities but Mudda f*er this book is SO worth it! It's fanf*ckingtastic!<br><br>This phenomenal installment made me feel on the verge all the time. I've been bombarded with too many things at the same time - clockwise and counter clockwise. I thought I would come out of my skin reading each pages!<br><br><b> The Hero and Heroine </b><br><br>This sequel showcased Thanatos (sexy SEXY Than), the fourth horseman also called Death if his Seal breaks. <br><br>I don't have the hots for this actor but as soon as Than was mentioned in the first book. His image danced non stop in my head. And I must add he fits Thanatos (for me anyways)<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1435038513i/15293442.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Our heroine Regan. Exteriorly bad ass Aegi guardian but interiorly scarred and scared from not being wanted and needed by her adopted family who at the end (most of them) majorly screwed her over.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1435038513i/15293443.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I've been wanting to read Than's story. And I was lucky that even though I maybe one of the readers out there that just started this series I can just breeze through em - no waiting game. Win win.<br><br><br><b> NOTE TO ALL THE READERS: THAN IS MINE! </b><br>He intrigued me to no end. From his aloofness and quietness to his tats, it's like he's beckoning me to come up and lick him clean. I'm a real sucker for Romeos like him. He is several layers of himself piled up. And with every layer I peeled, I've gotten to know him in the deepest level...and these layers unknowingly crawled and burrowed under my skin making him my favourite rider. Oh and he likes reading too *squeaks* like me!<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1435038513i/15293444.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> The STORY </b><br><br>Their story actually began in book 2 when Regan accepted the assignment that was given by Aegie elders where she marched up to Than's house and forced herself to live with him - giving him the excuse that he would need her special abilities but really her ulterior motive was to take advantage of him to fall pregnant .<br>I had no strong feelings towards her. I didn't hate her nor did I like her character. But in this installment I sympathized with her. How she gotten to know the real Than and regretted her motive. <br><br>This installment also showed how they fought their growing feelings for each other esp Than and boy did I like every single of it! He was so new to this game that this very bad and dangerous horseman turned into blubbering idiot and his reluctance was very VERY endearing.<br><br>I was so touched how he looks after Regan and his unborn child<br><i> “Not too much,” Than said quickly. “Just the basics. I want to buy the other stuff myself.” Man, he was going to look like a fool in Babies “R” Us, wasn’t he? “And…” He trailed off, his cheeks heating. “And could you get some lotion? Something pregnant women use for stretch marks? And back rubs?” </i><br><br>But cringed and hung head in frustration when he gives her snide comments<br><i> “Maybe you should have thought about that before you forced me to fuck you.” </i><br><br>His naïveté made me LOL with hand slaps on the thigh at the same time <br><i> “But she’s having … what are they called? Breaking Dicks?”<br>“Braxton Hicks,” Shade muttered.” </i><br><br>And when they finally act on their feelings - made me blushed and squirmed with delight <br><i> “Desk?” she whispered against his lips.<br>“We are so on the same page,” he whispered back.” </i><br><br>****Oi! make that: we SO are ALL on the same page - yes, I included myself! Coz I was so anticipating this very damn thing to happen****<br><br>Heart squeezed when I saw his vulnerability <br><i> “Don’t take her from me, Reaver.” </i><br><br>And laugh again with his overprotectiveness <br><i> Thanatos cursed. “Are they dead?”<br>“No.”<br>“Do you want them to be?”<br>She laughed. Thanatos definitely took his Horseman name to heart.” </i><br><br>And finally, FINALLY the admission!<br><i> “Yeah, I get it, okay, Regan? I get that you fucked me for the sake of the world. You did it in hopes that you’d save billions of lives. But you know what? I don’t care. I’m probably the only male on the planet who didn’t want to get used for sex. Who didn’t want to be treated “like a piece of meat. Maybe that makes me a big damned pussy, but I don’t give a shit. I thought you wanted me like I wanted you.” </i><br><br>****I kissed my e-book reader for this SH*T! Such momentous moment! And people on the train distanced themselves upon seeing my craziness. Ha! They don't know what their missing out!<br><br><br><b> The GOOD </b> (heroes in this sequel)<br>Reaver - you truly are the good guardian of the horsemen.<br><br>Limos - for your wise words <br><i> “But I think I’d do whatever it took to make sure that being with me was what was best.” </i><br><br>Kynan - a true leader of Aegis<br><br>Wraith - for siding with the goodies<br><i> “ He jabbed his finger at Lance and bared his fangs. “You’re mine. And dude, I play with my food.” </i><br><br><br><b> The BAD </b> <br>~ Lance<br>~ Gethel<br>You two are grade A premium d*ck and biatch! I hope you both rot in hell!<br><br><br><b> The 50-50 </b> <br>Harvester<br><br><i> “Of all the Horsemen, he’s the one most in need.” </i><br><b> WAS </b> ~grins~ but not anymore.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1435038513i/15293445._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Verdict: <b> HIGHLY recommended! Highly recommended read! Highly recommend series! </b><br>Rating: 5 ++++ stars</span>

<div id="review_197468691" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/197468691" />
    <a title="Melanie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5176570-melanie"><img alt="Melanie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1337864692p2/5176570.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/197468691?book_show_action=true">Aug 11, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Melanie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Melanie" href="/user/show/5176570-melanie">Melanie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Mass Market Paperback 9780446574501" href="/book/show/13057150-lethal-rider">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5176570-melanie?shelf=demonica">demonica</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5176570-melanie?shelf=lickable-tattoos">lickable-tattoos</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5176570-melanie?shelf=bite-me">bite-me</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5176570-melanie?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5176570-melanie?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5176570-melanie?shelf=demons-do-it-for-me">demons-do-it-for-me</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5176570-melanie?shelf=frau-badass">frau-badass</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5176570-melanie?shelf=knocked-up">knocked-up</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5176570-melanie?shelf=apocalypse-now">apocalypse-now</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5176570-melanie?shelf=hey-look-what-i-can-do">hey-look-what-i-can-do</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer197468691" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13944573384252088029">I've been <s>addicted to</s>hooked on Ione's 'Demonica' world since first reading 'Pleasure Unbound'. Seriously steamy and well-written, I avidly devoured that series and immediately delved into her just-as-sexy apocalyptic spin-off 'Lords of Deliverance' books as they've been released. In fact, on official release day of 'Lethal Rider' I scoured the city frantically looking for a copy before finding one so I could proudly add it to my hard-copy collection (after reading it of course)! I know, I know -</span>
  <span id="freeText13944573384252088029" style="display:none">I've been <s>addicted to</s>hooked on Ione's 'Demonica' world since first reading 'Pleasure Unbound'. Seriously steamy and well-written, I avidly devoured that series and immediately delved into her just-as-sexy apocalyptic spin-off 'Lords of Deliverance' books as they've been released. In fact, on official release day of 'Lethal Rider' I scoured the city frantically looking for a copy before finding one so I could proudly add it to my hard-copy collection (after reading it of course)! I know, I know - I <i>could</i> have gotten the ebook or pre-ordered it, but all my others are hard-copy (and I'm neurotically fanatical about keeping my series in the same format) and you can bet your a$$ I've learned my lesson and will pre-order the next one!<br /><br />I'm not going to get into a synopsis of 'Lethal Rider' except to say this is the third book in the 'Lords of Deliverance' series about the Four Horsemen of the Apocalypse and (as one could guess from the title) this is Death/Thanatos' book. If you haven't read any of the 'Demonica/Lords of Deliverance' books (*gasp* say it ain't so!), <i>don't</i> start with this one, or even the first LOD. Start with Demonica #1 'Pleasure Unbound' - because a) LOD relies heavily on the Demonica world and b) it's <u>AWESOME</u>! <br /><br />Now onto 'Lethal Rider'! <br />What I liked: <br />1) Than. Since meeting the 4 Horsemen, I've always loved Than - as Death, Than is sinister, completely bada$$ and covered in tats, yet also vulnerable, tortured by his past and actions and was carnally innocent - hello, could the guy get any sexier? Hell, no! <br /><br />2) Regan. We first met Regan in the 'Immortal Rider' when she's sent on a mission by the Aegis to Than's keep. Poor girl - her job was to seduce Than, because there was a prophesy a child of Death's would save the world. Well, she manages to get the job done (although the circumstances are dubious at best) and we start LR with Regan 8.5 months pregnant and she's preggers most of the book. That is kinda cool!<br /><br />3) Than &amp; Regan. Sure these two have a rocky start - Regan stole Than's virginity (which was believed to be a huge apocalyptic no-no) and although they were both under the influence of an aphrodisiac/drug he was essentially raped. BUT when he (finally) finds out about "ponyboy", and learns the whole truth he does everything in his power to protect Regan and baby - <i>and</i> he never stopped desiring her! Anyone who's ever been pregnant (or is) knows how clunky you feel, especially in the later stages, so Than's randiness towards Regan despite and because of the pregnancy is more than kinda cool! This desire, of course, morphs into love (*sigh*). Regan, for her part, feels guilty about her actions and is incredibly accepting of Than - both of his past and <i>who</i> he is. <br /><br />4) Reaver and Harvester! This storyline, although it takes up (too) little page time, has been brewing since 'Eternal Rider' and almost stole the whole show. Especially after the the little short story <i>teaser</i> Ione gifted us with in 'Apocalypse: The Lords of Deliverance Compendium'. (*<i>Larissa - please stop teasing us!!! There's no denying this twist is <b>hugely</b> exciting - but I can't take it anymore!!</i>*) Their story, when we finally get it, is gonna be awesome. <br /><br />What I didn't like:<br />Well there wasn't much I didn't like, <i>but</i> there were few spots in the story that were just a bit too convoluted IMO and had me going: huh? When all was said and done, I got it (or forgot about it) and I'm a biased enough Larissa Ione fan that this issue didn't hinder my overall enjoyment of LR.<br /><br />I would say that 'Lethal Rider' is an amazing addition to the 'Demonica/LOD' series. The series story arc has definitely been pushed forward, things are starting to look up, and I can't wait to finally <i>meet</i> Reseph in 'Rogue Rider'. I've been looking forward to his book just as much as Reaver and Harvester's story! Ride on! <br /><br /><br /><br /> <br /><br /><br /><br /><br /> </span>
  <a data-text-id="13944573384252088029" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Neyra ♦" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6872601-neyra"><img alt="Neyra ♦" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442631049p2/6872601.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/271500363?book_show_action=true">Feb 02, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Neyra ♦" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Neyra ♦" href="/user/show/6872601-neyra">Neyra ♦</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6872601-neyra?shelf=best-of-2012">best-of-2012</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer271500363" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2521373971705474361">Absolutely amazing. The outcome far outweighed the expectations I had for <i>Lethal Rider</i>. <br/><br/>Of course it had it's flaws, but the joy I felt at every page while reading and anticipating what was to come next left me with little to no argument for whether they should affect my love of the series. They did not. Though, I was torn throughout the story for about 65% of the book, I finally decided to just simply put my emotions out of the way, and accept what had to be done.. I tried anyways, Lol. Still, </span>
  <span id="freeText2521373971705474361" style="display:none">Absolutely amazing. The outcome far outweighed the expectations I had for <i>Lethal Rider</i>. <br><br>Of course it had it's flaws, but the joy I felt at every page while reading and anticipating what was to come next left me with little to no argument for whether they should affect my love of the series. They did not. Though, I was torn throughout the story for about 65% of the book, I finally decided to just simply put my emotions out of the way, and accept what had to be done.. I tried anyways, Lol. Still, I loved it! <br><br>As we learned in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/9868970-immortal-rider" rel="nofollow noopener">Immortal Rider</a>, Regan manipulated her way into Thanatos' keep and ultimately accomplished her goal of seducing him. As Regan's betrayal rocked him and his fury escalated, Thanatos unleashed a death wave that resulted in casualties of the souls in his Greenland island, leaving Ares and Limos with no choice but to paralyze him with hellhound saliva. For eight months, Thanatos was stuck in his own mind, thinking of only ways to kill Regan, unbeknownst to him, she was preparing to deliver his child. When he's finally released from his prison, Than sets his eyes on finding Regan, and killing her. All the while, the apocalypse draws ever near with Pesitilence scheming to destroy the unborn baby.<br><br>I don't think I have to reiterate that I love Thanatos. It's a given x) His anger, pain, his rages. He's every bit Death, and every bit the sensual man he never thought he could be. He's also kind and considerate. But who knew, right? lol. I love how he was pissed and raging one minute, then he turns into a big ball of mush where his baby's concerned x) As for Regan, I like that he doesn't fall to his knees and does as she asks like a total fool. He stands his ground and refuses to budge. Shocking is an understatement, for a virgin, his mind works in extremely wicked ways. A sex slave to Than? Sign me up! ;D <br><br>Regan; okay I'll admit, no matter how many times I go back to reading <i>Lethal Rider</i>, I will never, <u>never</u> like Regan. I don't care how much she says she's sorry. Doesn't matter how much she did it "for the greater good", not even the fact that she feels remorse over her actions, <i>nothing</i> changes the fact that she betrayed Thanatos in the most unrefutably disgusting way. She manipulated, lied and wormed her way into his home, and used him! <br><br>Alright, my rant is through ^-^ Ultimately though, I still don't like her. She was arrogant, naive, and annoying. And not only that, but she kept blaming Thanatos at every turn for the casualties of her so-called "friends", which is bullfuckingshit, as Than likes to say :D I really wish Larissa had gone a different route where Thanatos' love interest was concerned, but what the hell. *shrugs* I really enjoyed reading the book.<br><br>In the midst of Than and Regan's fighting, they have Pestilence to deal with, betrayal at every turn of the worst kind, and The Aegis. Which will either shock you, or make you yell in an emotional outburst, " I knew it! " And the source of the chaos? Damn! That's all I'm going to say cause I sure as hell hadn't seen that one coming! ;) <br><br><b>Actual Rating:</b> I give this read a 4.5 because like I said, I believe the love interest should have gone a different route, but I'm not disappointed of the outcome at all :)<br><br><i>I received this book as an advanced reader copy by the publisher via netgalley</i>.<br><br><br><b>May 1, 2012:</b><br><br><i>
  <b>Just one month to go! <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/168063.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> Thanatos ♥ <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/93698.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> You're almost here! <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/93515.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> OH YEAH!! <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/96260.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> *Sigh*</b>
</i></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2278800-anzu-the-great-destroyer?shelf=holy-winged-ones">holy-winged-ones</a>,
