              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2278800-anzu-the-great-destroyer?shelf=romance-paranormal">romance-paranormal</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer190162186" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6073394031337606989"><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>From virgin to dad in zero to sixty.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br/><u>Long story short</u><br/>After stealing the virginity of Thanatos, fourth Horseman of the Apocalypse, Regan, an Aegis Guardian, gets pregnant and almost destroys the world. Thanatos wants to kill her because she lied to him in order to steal his <s>semen</s> virginity. Regan has the hots for Than. Than has the hots for Regan. The end.<br/><br/><u>My thoughts</u><br/>I was extremely unhappy with the fact that Regan is pregnant in <i>Lethal Rider</i> because I could not stand the thought of goi</span>
  <span id="freeText6073394031337606989" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>From virgin to dad in zero to sixty.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><u>Long story short</u><br>After stealing the virginity of Thanatos, fourth Horseman of the Apocalypse, Regan, an Aegis Guardian, gets pregnant and almost destroys the world. Thanatos wants to kill her because she lied to him in order to steal his <s>semen</s> virginity. Regan has the hots for Than. Than has the hots for Regan. The end.<br><br><u>My thoughts</u><br>I was extremely unhappy with the fact that Regan is pregnant in <i>Lethal Rider</i> because I could not stand the thought of going through a pregnancy-related book. Lucky for me the book wasn’t that bad.<br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380354595i/707355._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Larissa Ione is very good with entertaining the bored reader. When she isn’t writing about chastity belts, that is. When she writes about pregnant Aegis Guardians and Death, she gets pretty good.<br><br>Have no fear, <i>Lethal Rider</i> has the typical Paranormal Romance moments. For example, Regan fucked Than, pun intended, and his punishment is to force her to have sex with him ever night.<br><blockquote>
<i>Slutty Student</i>: “ I’ve been a bad bad student.”<br><i>Perv Professor</i>: “Well then I’ll just have to punish you a bit. Bend over so I can spank your perky ass.”</blockquote><br>Makes total sense.<br><br>Anywho, apart from these stupid, if I may call them that, scenes <i>Lethal Rider</i> was a decent read. It went on fast and I didn’t feel the need to gouge out my eyes or vomit because of too much sweetness.<br><br>Oh, and by the way, am I the only one who envisions Pestilence as looking like Loki? <br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380354595ra/707356.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><u>To read or not to read?</u><br>I would recommend <i>Lethal Rider</i> to those who have already read the previous <i>Lords of Deliverance</i> books. If you have read the<i>Demonica</i> series, even better. If you have no idea what I’m talking about, then I suggest you start either with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8843801.Eternal_Rider__Lords_of_Deliverance___1_" title="Eternal Rider (Lords of Deliverance, #1) by Larissa Ione" rel="nofollow noopener"> Eternal Rider</a> or <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/2679633.Pleasure_Unbound__Demonica___1_" title="Pleasure Unbound (Demonica, #1) by Larissa Ione" rel="nofollow noopener"> Pleasure Unbound</a>. The story in <i>Lethal Rider</i> is tightly related to these books, and you’ll be lost like a cheerleader at Comic-Con if you don’t allow yourself to be properly introduced to Larissa Ione’s universe.<br><br><u>Favorite quote</u><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“Obviously,” Than said, “she’s better. No thanks to you. But she’s having … what are they called? Breaking Dicks?” <br>“Braxton Hicks,” Shade muttered.</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><b>3.5 stars</b><br><br>Review also posted on<br><a href="http://zombiehazard.blogspot.com/2012/10/lethal-rider-lords-of-deliverance-3.html" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380340428i/696822.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<div id="review_238152769" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/238152769" />
    <a title="Ezinwanyi Chinyere" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4386752-ezinwanyi-chinyere"><img alt="Ezinwanyi Chinyere" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1600017870p2/4386752.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/238152769?book_show_action=true">Nov 21, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ezinwanyi Chinyere" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ezinwanyi Chinyere" href="/user/show/4386752-ezinwanyi-chinyere">Ezinwanyi Chinyere</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4386752-ezinwanyi-chinyere?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4386752-ezinwanyi-chinyere?shelf=magic">magic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4386752-ezinwanyi-chinyere?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4386752-ezinwanyi-chinyere?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4386752-ezinwanyi-chinyere?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer238152769" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17911860696469016003">This one starts right where Immortal Riders ended, with Thanatos (fourth horseman of the Apocalypse) in the induced comatose state. He is being kept there by his siblings, since his anger and its consequences are renowned. If you remember from the previous book, Thanatos had just discovered Regan’s duplicitous action and he was raging. Limos & Ares decided to buy time and figure out how to deal with Pestilence while hoping Thanatos’ wrath will subside. <br/><br/>After eight and a half months, Thanatos’ pa</span>
  <span id="freeText17911860696469016003" style="display:none">This one starts right where Immortal Riders ended, with Thanatos (fourth horseman of the Apocalypse) in the induced comatose state. He is being kept there by his siblings, since his anger and its consequences are renowned. If you remember from the previous book, Thanatos had just discovered Regan’s duplicitous action and he was raging. Limos &amp; Ares decided to buy time and figure out how to deal with Pestilence while hoping Thanatos’ wrath will subside. <br /><br />After eight and a half months, Thanatos’ paralysis wore off before his next dose of hellhound saliva, and he escaped. He goes after the Aegi guardian, Reagan Matthews, whom he believes betrayed him. He tracked her to an Aegi headquarter and he kidnaps her. Initially he planned to force her to compensate him for the lost eight months by being his beckon and call girl. She must fulfill his every sexual desire at his every whim. But upon returning to his keep, Thanatos discovers that Regan is pregnant with his child, and worse, she plans on giving their child, Thanatos’ agimortus, away.<br /><br />Thanatos is forced to reexamine his desire for revenge. Is it worth giving up the one thing he has always desired, a child and a family of his own? Is it even possible to form a family with a woman that he believes untrustworthy and loyal to the wrong people? Finally, how will he deal with Pestilence (Respesh), who wants to kill the baby as soon as it is born and the pending apocalypse?<br /><br />This book was my favorite of the Lord of Deliverance series. It was packed with action, great dialogue, emotional highs and lows. It was wrought with sexual tension as well as romance. It was dark, yet full of humor. It was everything a great book ought to be. Ione did a great job fleshing out Regan’s character, her OCD behaviors and her private pain. It allowed us to understand Regan and her relationship with the Aegi. She also made Thanatos into one of my favorite heroes. He is so damaged, yet compassionate. As the Rider of Death, he seems so cold, deadly and lethal, but he actually is the most fragile of the horsemen. He was in so much pain, that it was hard not to sympathize with him. It was a joy to observe how he opened himself up to the possibility of having a family. I just couldn’t put this book down. I loved this book and I can’t wait for the next one.<br /><br />At the end of this book was a preview for Rogue Rider, but I didn’t read it. I can’t take the teasing. I will wait until the entire novel is ready. Larissa Ione is definitely one of my favorite authors.<br /><br />I strongly recommend, actually I insist that you must read the Demonica series, all five books in order before starting the Lord of Deliverance series. Eidolon, Shade, Wraith, Lore and Sin all make appearances with their mates. Their history will help you understand their talents and gifts. <br /><br /><br />I LOVED THIS INSTALLMENT! <br /><br />***e-arc received from Netgalley***</span>
  <a data-text-id="17911860696469016003" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer6987161668389429137">This is a Quickie Review. For the full review, please visit <a href='http://romanceaholic.com/2012/release-review-lethal-rider-larissa-ione/' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Romanceaholic</a>. Please note the full review contains spoilers for previous novels in the series. <br/><br/>Expected Release Date: May 22, 2012<br/>Publisher: Grand Central Publishing<br/>Imprint: Forever<br/>Author’s Website: <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://larissaione.com'>http://larissaione.com</a><br/>My Source for This Book: Netgalley<br/>Part of a Series: Yes, Book 3, Lords of Deliverance (Spinoff of the Demonica Series)<br/>Series Best Read In Order: Yes<br/>Steam Level: Steamy<br/><br/>I've been a fan of the Demonica Series, and sub</span>
  <span id="freeText6987161668389429137" style="display:none">This is a Quickie Review. For the full review, please visit <a href="http://romanceaholic.com/2012/release-review-lethal-rider-larissa-ione/" rel="nofollow noopener">The Romanceaholic</a>. Please note the full review contains spoilers for previous novels in the series. <br /><br />Expected Release Date: May 22, 2012<br />Publisher: Grand Central Publishing<br />Imprint: Forever<br />Author’s Website: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://larissaione.com">http://larissaione.com</a><br />My Source for This Book: Netgalley<br />Part of a Series: Yes, Book 3, Lords of Deliverance (Spinoff of the Demonica Series)<br />Series Best Read In Order: Yes<br />Steam Level: Steamy<br /><br />I've been a fan of the Demonica Series, and subsequently the Lords of Deliverance Series since their inception, and this book is no exception. Full of action, drama, steamy romance, and terrifying plot twists, I was happy to see that Than and Regan still had the same intense chemistry that we'd witnessed between them in Immortal Rider.<br /><br />The main thing keeping this book from being a 5-star read was simply the fact that as Book 3 of a spin-off of another 5-Book series, it tends to be a case of "more of the same". While I was glad to see that certain long-standing elements of the series-wide story arc were resolved, I admit that there were several instances where I was tempted to skim over parts that were feeling a bit repetitive. Also, since Than and Regan's story began in the previous book, much of the early story was spent rehashing the dramatic and even traumatic way that Regan got pregnant to being with.<br /><br />That said, I loved them as a couple. Regan and Thanatos are easily my favorite couple of the Lords of Deliverance series, and I was very pleased to see so much of the delicious chemistry and snarky by-play that I'd enjoyed so much in Immortal Rider.<br /><br />I admit that I was a little disappointed that we didn't get more background on Reaver and Harvester, but they played a big enough part to keep me from protesting TOO loudly (not to mention the setup for the next book!).<br /><br />I do, of course, think that this story is best suited for those who have already read, at bare minimum, the previous book in the series, simply because there is so much history that newcomers will either be totally lost, or miss out on the significance of many of the story's developments.<br /><br />While this is not my favorite title by Larissa Ione, I can easily say it's my favorite installment of the Lords of Deliverance series, and as such is very firmly on my keeper shelf.<br /><br />A solid 4.5/5 Stars<br /><br />Lords of Deliverance Series Reading Order:<br />* Eternal Rider <br />* Vampire Fight Club (Novella in the Supernatural anthology)<br />* Immortal Rider <br />* Lethal Rider <br />* Apocalypse: the Lords of Deliverance Compendium <br /> </span>

<div id="review_191269934" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="Ronda  Tutt" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2216375-ronda-tutt"><img alt="Ronda  Tutt" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1475858100p2/2216375.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/191269934?book_show_action=true">Jul 28, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ronda  Tutt" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ronda  Tutt" href="/user/show/2216375-ronda-tutt">Ronda  Tutt</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Mass Market Paperback 9780446574501" href="/book/show/13057150-lethal-rider">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer191269934" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1995076485933366115">Heart Throbbing Exciting!<br/><br/>What a brilliant story! I love this author, she has weave a story that captures your heart in a thrilling world wind drama between good and evil. I love the fact that evil is not necessary bad/evil. <br/><br/>I love Than and think he is what a perfect man should be, Handsome, Charming, Sexy, Built, Tough, Bad Boy, and an Ass at times but an ass that is humorous and sincere when you least expect it. He's deadly and dangerous but tender and sweet when it's called for.<br/><br/>The characters </span>
  <span id="freeText1995076485933366115" style="display:none">Heart Throbbing Exciting!<br /><br />What a brilliant story! I love this author, she has weave a story that captures your heart in a thrilling world wind drama between good and evil. I love the fact that evil is not necessary bad/evil. <br /><br />I love Than and think he is what a perfect man should be, Handsome, Charming, Sexy, Built, Tough, Bad Boy, and an Ass at times but an ass that is humorous and sincere when you least expect it. He's deadly and dangerous but tender and sweet when it's called for.<br /><br />The characters connection between Than and Regan was heart warming electrifying and so hot! The tenderness and passion Than showed Regan even with her being pregnant was so emotionally beautiful.<br /><br />The plot of the story kept me glued to the pages and the words flowed and visually came alive for me in color as if I was watching a movie. The excitement and action packed events between the games of evil Reseph played upon his siblings and the betrayal of the Aegis kept me on the edge of my seat. One word comes to mind about this series and that is the word - Addicting! <br /><br />I always loved the new findings and clues the author gives us towards solving the myth/lore about keeping the Apocalypse from starting and how to keep the horsemen's seal from breaking. Between the legendary Daemonica and the Holy Bible, the fight for truth and interpretation of the scriptures makes the story even more mysterious.<br /><br />The ending was perfect, my emotions were running wild in the end and had me nearly in tears of sadness and tears of joy and then a surprising holy shit revelation about Reseph and the knife Deliverance.<br /><br />All the secondary characters added fun and humorous excitement to the story and made me want a hellhound - LOL I totally loved this book and I highly recommend everyone to read this series or actually any of Larissa Ione's books. She is truely a gifted and talented writer and I'm a true fan. Now I am patiently waiting for the 4th book in the series to come out "Rogue Rider".<br /><br />Excellent Read! <br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="1995076485933366115" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer9575086591278250031">We find out that Regan was tricked into drugging Thanatos and herself which helped her complete the plan of having sex with him and getting pregnant. Thanatos is beyond livid not only from losing his virginity but from being essentially raped. Ares and Limos felt it was best to keep him paralyzed with hellhound saliva so he doesn't kill anymore than he already has. The problem is Thanatos doesn't know Regan is pregnant and all hell is about to break loose! <br/><br/>Well, I was sooo looking forward to thi</span>
  <span id="freeText9575086591278250031" style="display:none">We find out that Regan was tricked into drugging Thanatos and herself which helped her complete the plan of having sex with him and getting pregnant. Thanatos is beyond livid not only from losing his virginity but from being essentially raped. Ares and Limos felt it was best to keep him paralyzed with hellhound saliva so he doesn't kill anymore than he already has. The problem is Thanatos doesn't know Regan is pregnant and all hell is about to break loose! <br /><br />Well, I was sooo looking forward to this book and I hate to say that I'm a bit disappointed. I'm partly to blame as I was hoping there would be much more angst but unfortunately, there isn't. Both Than and Regan <i>quickly</i> and <i>pretty easily</i> forgave each other. Than was especially shocking! I felt they needed more time to work things out and just more "alone" time. <br /><br />I do have to say that I really like both of them. I've always liked Than and he is even more endearing in this book. (Loved the cradle and vampire porn!) I was surprised to like Regan and I think a lot of it had to do with her coming to terms with her becoming a Mom. (Loved the OCD moments too.) <br /><br />We get a lot of interaction from mostly all the past characters. (not enough Wraith though!) Some good insight into Reaver and Harvester...enough that it makes you want to read their book NOW. Have to say that I figured out the ploy with Gethel although her reasoning's were a bit surprising. <br /><br />And wow...what can u say about Reseph aka Pestilence? He is seriously one bada$$! The part at the end in the cave is pretty heart wrenching and I liked how LI threw that little curve ball. I don't want to set myself up ~ again ~ but I don't know how he's going to work through what he's done. Can't wait to find out! <br /><br />Favorite quotes: <br /><br />♦ She turned to him, her cheeks burning red. “What is this? Vampire porn?” <br /><br />“Yep.” <br /><br />“Oh, and this is a good one. Muffy the Vampire Layer.”<br /><br /><br />♥ “For the next eight and a half months, you're going to be mine. Every. Night.”<br /><br /></span>

<div id="review_325289529" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/325289529" />
    <a title="Brittany B." class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4862342-brittany-b"><img alt="Brittany B." src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1344335511p2/4862342.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/325289529?book_show_action=true">May 06, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Brittany B." class="user" itemprop="url" name="Brittany B." href="/user/show/4862342-brittany-b">Brittany B.</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Mass Market Paperback 9780446574501" href="/book/show/13057150-lethal-rider">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4862342-brittany-b?shelf=great-series">great-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4862342-brittany-b?shelf=rom_pnr">rom_pnr</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer325289529" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17076945126272214514"><b>4.5 Stars</b> <br/><br/>A great book. Fabulous addition to a Kick-Ass series!! <br/><br/>I think this series itself is better than any one book. Larissa Ione has woven an amazing tapestry full of depth, passion, peril and excitement with this series. Each book adds to the whole world she's created, making the series absolutely more addictive than any other series I've read lately, except for KMM's Fever books. I seriously give the books my highest recommendation. <br/><br/>Not to say this book was perfect. Larissa Ione has a hab</span>
  <span id="freeText17076945126272214514" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Stars</b> <br /><br />A great book. Fabulous addition to a Kick-Ass series!! <br /><br />I think this series itself is better than any one book. Larissa Ione has woven an amazing tapestry full of depth, passion, peril and excitement with this series. Each book adds to the whole world she's created, making the series absolutely more addictive than any other series I've read lately, except for KMM's Fever books. I seriously give the books my highest recommendation. <br /><br />Not to say this book was perfect. Larissa Ione has a habit of ending her books with cheesy lines. I noticed that in Demonica, and the scene that immediately comes to mind is from Sin Undone. Kynan's words after Jem gives birth and it's time to name their baby girl: (not a direct quote, but close enough to give the cheesy gist) <i>She's my sun. You (Jem) are my world. This is my dawn...Oh let's call the baby Dawn.</i> <br />Similarly, there was definitely some super-cheese at the very end of the book causing serious eye-rolling action. But I can live with that! <br /><br />I really liked the story between Regan and Thanatos. I didnt think Lethal Rider was quite as exciting as book 2, though it picked up tremendously in the second half. I liked the second book because so much action was going on with all the characters. It wasn't all about Limos and Arik. This book was more PNR, focusing on the main couple. Also, so much of the exciting setup for the Regan/Thanatos plot happened in the previous book. Regardless, the book really was excellent, and I can't say much more or I'll definitely spoil the plot. I will give Larissa Ione credit for not dragging her plots on. These books have action and resolution. The next book will deal with the wild, unexpected resolution and outcome of this one, and it will be a new world for many characters. I'm so excited to read it. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="17076945126272214514" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_318157607" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/318157607" />
    <a title="MISS VAIN" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4335141-miss-vain"><img alt="MISS VAIN" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1312749379p2/4335141.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/318157607?book_show_action=true">Apr 24, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="MISS VAIN" class="user" itemprop="url" name="MISS VAIN" href="/user/show/4335141-miss-vain">MISS VAIN</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4335141-miss-vain?shelf=larissa-ione">larissa-ione</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4335141-miss-vain?shelf=series-that-i-m-obsessed-with">series-that-i-m-obsessed-with</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4335141-miss-vain?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4335141-miss-vain?shelf=sizzling-pnr">sizzling-pnr</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4335141-miss-vain?shelf=hes-in-my-harem">hes-in-my-harem</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4335141-miss-vain?shelf=war-gods">war-gods</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer318157607" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8864446670409014000"><b>And she remembered the expression on his face when he realized she'd betrayed him. She was going to die, and it would all have been for nothing.</b><br/><br/>Lethal Rider begins eight months after Regan betrayed Thanatos in Eternal Rider.  Poor Thanatos has been living such a horrific life these past eight months sedated by Hellhound saliva rendering him in a bed unable to move at his siblings request. They believe they're doing what is best for his safety as well as the safety of those around him with the th</span>
  <span id="freeText8864446670409014000" style="display:none"><b>And she remembered the expression on his face when he realized she'd betrayed him. She was going to die, and it would all have been for nothing.</b><br /><br />Lethal Rider begins eight months after Regan betrayed Thanatos in Eternal Rider.  Poor Thanatos has been living such a horrific life these past eight months sedated by Hellhound saliva rendering him in a bed unable to move at his siblings request. They believe they're doing what is best for his safety as well as the safety of those around him with the threat of the apocalypse. Oddly enough he hates Regan with such a fierce passion yet he yearns for her with the same amount of passion. Each passing day of these eight months have been torture. When he's not spending the day watching television he's either plotting Regan's death or in visioning himself satisfying her in bed. *Sigh* talk about a steamy situation. <br /><br /><b>Why had she gone to extremes to get him in bed. Legend, he might have starfucker appeal, and sure, he knew he was handsome but resorting to drugs her supernatural ability in order to get what she wanted? </b><br /><br />Regan has been regretting her actions since she first realized that Thanatos would make good on his promise to kill her. Over time as she is stuck at Aegis headquarters awaiting the birth of her child that has been prophesied as to the key to ending the Apocalypse. She has decided to give her child a home full of love that can provide a safer environment than Regan feels she can. Though she plans to place her child in the home of Kynan and Gem, Larissa Ione gives us little glimpses into Regan's slight apprehension, not because she doesn't feel they would fully provide for her child, but she has been bonding with the tiny life that is growing inside of her and her maternal instincts are developing. <br /><br /><b>"Then why did you save me?"<br />"Save you?" The vampire gestured to the ashy mess that used to be his brethren. "He was merely here to kill you. I'm taking you to Thanatos." He grinned. "Trust me, I didn't save you."</b><br /><br />However the warrior Thanatos has other plans that may disrupt Regan's because his plans are to devour Regan one way or another he will have her under his control sooner rather than later. He soon discovers that he can move his legs, so he plans to outwit his siblings and forgo the next dose of Hellhound Saliva so he can get out from under their control and begin taking control of his life again, little does he know that Regan and his siblings have been hiding this pregnancy from him leaving him stunned. <br /><br />From here Thanatos becomes the horseman we all know him as; fierce, sexy and Alpha! This revelation of soon becoming a father has him rethinking his desire to kill Regan but to protect her at least until the baby is born. He has always desired a family, and slowly we see an incredibly sexy side of Thanatos, where one minute he's angry, the next he's aroused, and then ready to take down an army to protect what is rightfully his. He's greedy with his possessions and I found that intoxicating. <br /><br /><b>"Is everything okay?" Ares's voice came from the end of the hallway. "Limos is nursing on a headache, and Arik wants to shove an M-80 up your ass." "Kinky," Than said, "but I'm new to the sex thing. I'm not ready for hardcore yet." </b><br /><br />This book also has plenty of sub plots that have me anxious to dive right into the next book. Between Reseph aka Pestilence being his usual bastard self you can't help but love him as a super villain. I believe his book will touch our hearts the most because he's going to have a rough road ahead with his new alter ego Pestilence running the show. I'm excited just thinking about it. I enjoyed Reaver and all his escapades, he leaves me with a soft spot in my heart. Probably the most exciting reunion would be the cameos we get with the wonderful men of Underworld General  Hospital. <br /><br /><b>"You know what, buddy?" Wraith said. "They aren't worth it. Not now. But later...." He jabbed his finger at Lance and bared his fangs. "You're mine. And dude, I play with my food."</b><br /><br />I don't want to give anything away but this book contains many engaging plots as well mysteries are being unravelled slowly but gradually in each book and there were a couple mysteries solved in this book that made my jaw drop. I devoured this book in almost one setting which I was disappointed in myself because now I must wait for the next release. For fans of Larissa Ione, Lethal Rider will leave you satisfied in more ways than one. <br />This book is a must read for all paranormal romance lovers that enjoy and original engaging plot, mystery, and simply delicious passionate sex! Bravo to Larissa Ione. If I wasn't already a fan girl of her writing I would be now because her books are ridiculously  addicting. Is there an Ione support group for fans that simply can't get enough of her amazing paranormal writing skills?! If so, enroll me now!! ;)<br /><br /><b>"All I could think of was you. When I was gone, all I wanted was to be back here with you. Only you."</b><br /><br /><br /><br /><b>ARC</b> provided for review by <b>Netgalley</b><br /><br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://MissVainsParanormalFantasy.com">http://MissVainsParanormalFantasy.com</a><br /><br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="8864446670409014000" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2451459-nisha?shelf=pregnant-or-mothers">pregnant-or-mothers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2451459-nisha?shelf=angels-and-demons">angels-and-demons</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2451459-nisha?shelf=mythology">mythology</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2451459-nisha?shelf=kickass-heroine">kickass-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2451459-nisha?shelf=frenemies">frenemies</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2451459-nisha?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2451459-nisha?shelf=virgin-hero">virgin-hero</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer213217349" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14655638065422476054">I'm done with this book, but just being a sloth about getting my review written up and posted. <br/>--<br/>So naturally, it took me more than a week to get back to writing this review. It's the longest I've gone, but I think it has to do with writing a review that would do the book justice. I can't promise that even now, but I figure, I might as well try. <br/><br/>Anyone who has reached Lethal Rider, the 3rd book in the Lords of Deliverance series, is a fan of Ms. Ione. But I would bet my life, that compared to th</span>
  <span id="freeText14655638065422476054" style="display:none">I'm done with this book, but just being a sloth about getting my review written up and posted. <br />--<br />So naturally, it took me more than a week to get back to writing this review. It's the longest I've gone, but I think it has to do with writing a review that would do the book justice. I can't promise that even now, but I figure, I might as well try. <br /><br />Anyone who has reached Lethal Rider, the 3rd book in the Lords of Deliverance series, is a fan of Ms. Ione. But I would bet my life, that compared to the Demonica series, the Lords has been a little... less compelling (not exactly bad, since I still love reading her books more than any other PNR, just relatively...meh). But, that's because when we started reading the series, we knew the most exciting characters were Thanatos and Reseph. Surprise, surprise, when I tell you that Than's book (this book) is the best, so far, at least. <br /><br />So, Than is the Horseman of Death, and in book 2, lost his virginity to Regan, an Aegis. Their moment of lust seems to be contrived by <s>Reseph</s> Pestilence, in hopes that his seal would be broken. It doesn't break, but it creates Than's seal, his unborn son. Since Than has been guarding his virginity like it's the most precious thing in his life for centuries, he starts raging and destroying things in the way only Death can. Ares and Limos are forced to subdue him with hellhound venom stuff for 8 months. This book starts with the very pregnant Regan and the recently-escaped-from-paralytic-imprisonment, Thanatos. Than is compelled to protect his unborn son, which unfortunately means dragging around Regan, who he's still angry with and lusting after. Anyway, more drama happens, as Regan and Than fight their attraction, Pestilence is fucking up the world, and the Aegis creates new ways to screw over Team human/good demon/good horsemen. Oh yea, and Reaver secretly saves the world (*drool* I love you Reaver *fangirl squeal*). So, using deductive reasoning about the last book, we can deduce that it will be Reseph's book, since he is the last horseman, which means Than destroys Pestilence in this book. <i>Does that really sound like a spoiler to ya'll? I don't think so</i> Anyway, I am just so ready for the next book. I can't wait.<br /><br />So, one of the reasons why Lethal Rider is awesome is because both Than and Regan are just so badass. Their chemistry could have burned off the pages, if I hadn't read it on my kindle. Regan, I'm not going to elaborate. We all know she's pretty tough. Than, whoa, that man has a whole lotta baggage, literally. It really sucks to be Than, but he's kinda an ass sometimes, so you could see it coming. We get to see more of our favorite characters from Demonica - though, not always under the pink lenses from the Demonica series. The Horsemen aren't particularly fond of the Sem bros. We also get more of Reaver, which is awesome because he's my favorite character. I wonder if he'll get his own book. Probably not, but one could hope.<br /><br />My favorite part is Regan's nickname for her unborn son, <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Ponyboy. Get it? A Horseman's offspring can only be a "pony" "boy". <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />Overall, this was an amazing read. I can highly recommend it to anyone I know. If you like PNR and Ms. Ione's work, this would be stuck in your favorites shelf forever. It's good stuff. </span>
  <a data-text-id="14655638065422476054" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Francesca the Fierce (Under the Covers Book Blog)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3108364-francesca-the-fierce-under-the-covers-book-blog"><img alt="Francesca the Fierce (Under the Covers Book Blog)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1595947372p2/3108364.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/174640194?book_show_action=true">Jun 07, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Francesca the Fierce (Under the Covers Book Blog)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Francesca the Fierce (Under the Covers Book Blog)" href="/user/show/3108364-francesca-the-fierce-under-the-covers-book-blog">Francesca the Fierce (Under the Covers Book Blog)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Mass Market Paperback 9780446574501" href="/book/show/13057150-lethal-rider">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3108364-francesca-the-fierce-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3108364-francesca-the-fierce-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=books-read-2012">books-read-2012</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3108364-francesca-the-fierce-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=genre-paranormal-romance">genre-paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3108364-francesca-the-fierce-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=angels-demons">angels-demons</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer174640194" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6017378118897750234"><b>This review was posted at <a href='http://underthecoversbookblog.blogspot.com/2012/05/arc-review-lethal-rider-by-larissa-ione.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>Under the Covers</a></b><br/><br/>This has been a highly anticipated book for me. We are getting close to the Apocalypse, will they be able to prevent it or will all hell literally break loose?<br/>At the end of Immortal Rider Regan, a member of the Aegi, had volunteered to have sex with Thanatos and get pregnant. The whole thing went down with all kinds of betrayal and I couldn't help but feel like beating Regan to a pulp by the end of that book.<br/><br/>Lethal Rider starts eight and a half months la</span>
  <span id="freeText6017378118897750234" style="display:none"><b>This review was posted at <a href="http://underthecoversbookblog.blogspot.com/2012/05/arc-review-lethal-rider-by-larissa-ione.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Under the Covers</a></b><br /><br />This has been a highly anticipated book for me. We are getting close to the Apocalypse, will they be able to prevent it or will all hell literally break loose?<br />At the end of Immortal Rider Regan, a member of the Aegi, had volunteered to have sex with Thanatos and get pregnant. The whole thing went down with all kinds of betrayal and I couldn't help but feel like beating Regan to a pulp by the end of that book.<br /><br />Lethal Rider starts eight and a half months later. Regan is very much pregnant and in the custody of the Aegis and Thanatos has been in a hellhound saliva induced frozen state for that whole time, not knowing Regan was pregnant. When the hellhound saliva wears off before it should and he's able to escape and goes straight for that pull he has towards Regan, he finds it's not just her, she's carrying his child, so he kidnaps her to bring her to his home and keep her safe until she gives birth to his agimortus, or baby.<br /><br />I know some people are thinking "How could I be ok with her after what she did?" and I admit I felt a little bit like that but I understood her reasons why in this book perfectly. It's her past, the way she views herself and her relations with others and her loyalty to maybe the wrong people. I thought it was great that Thanatos took his time getting past that and it wasn't a magical "everything is ok now" moment. And of course, this is Thanatos we are talking about. Sexy bad boy, I just can't get enough of him!<br /><br />What a rollercoaster of destruction and mayhem everywhere! The land down under has been taken over by hell, Pestilence is causing so much chaos everywhere, getting allies in all the wrong places, and destroying everything in his path.<br /><br />What can you expect? Some things are not what they seem, angels, Aegi and vampires will throw you for a loop. Seems like you can't trust anyone! I loved seeing some of the past of Reseph's life, it wasn't much but it showed a caring side to him, and I admit I had to laugh at his music preferences! I feel this started setting him up as a character that we should like.<br /><br />There are also some minor and major clues about the origin of the horsemen so watch out for the clues in this book, as well as more information about the daywalker vampires and Thanatos role in their existence.<br /><br />There's just enough of the secondary characters that I love. Kynan, Wraith, Shade, Eidolon, Conan, Limos, and even a bit of Arik. I can't help but love that Ms. Ione keeps her old characters present and involved in her series.<br /><br />So am I ready for Reseph now? Since I won't tell you what happens in this book, then I can only say after this one, you'll only want to get Rogue Rider that much faster!!! <br /> <br />*ARC provided by publisher</span>
  <a data-text-id="6017378118897750234" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3988019-goge-barrons-le-moning-maniac?shelf=books-i-own">books-i-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3988019-goge-barrons-le-moning-maniac?shelf=lost-interest-alot-alittle-sumwhat">lost-interest-alot-alittle-sumwhat</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3988019-goge-barrons-le-moning-maniac?shelf=i-cried-wanna-make-something-of-it">i-cried-wanna-make-something-of-it</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3988019-goge-barrons-le-moning-maniac?shelf=lovable-hero">lovable-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3988019-goge-barrons-le-moning-maniac?shelf=series-continuing-update">series-continuing-update</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3988019-goge-barrons-le-moning-maniac?shelf=down-memory-lane">down-memory-lane</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3988019-goge-barrons-le-moning-maniac?shelf=stalled">stalled</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3988019-goge-barrons-le-moning-maniac?shelf=h-in-a-rut-cuz-hes-fallen-already">h-in-a-rut-cuz-hes-fallen-already</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3988019-goge-barrons-le-moning-maniac?shelf=on-shelf-i-have-it-will-read-it">on-shelf-i-have-it-will-read-it</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3988019-goge-barrons-le-moning-maniac?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer270685466" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4360861195638435347">SPOILERSSSSSSSSSSSSS<br/><br/><br/>||| UPDATE: After the steam died some, I find I must make my review less full of hate. I apologize for my emotions. |||<br/><br/><br/>I do want to read (finish) Thanatos's story. I DO!<br/><br/>...<br/><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385399136ra/7140920.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>But she is such a.. heroine who everyone treats like god, a delicate princess, perfect and gentle and a good  person all-around that the full-of-nonsense bull pricks me with anger-releasing emotions and frustrated hate. The generosity of the attention given to this heroine who I loathe blocks me from being </span>
  <span id="freeText4360861195638435347" style="display:none">SPOILERSSSSSSSSSSSSS<br><br><br>||| UPDATE: After the steam died some, I find I must make my review less full of hate. I apologize for my emotions. |||<br><br><br>I do want to read (finish) Thanatos's story. I DO!<br><br>...<br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385399136ra/7140920.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>But she is such a.. heroine who everyone treats like god, a delicate princess, perfect and gentle and a good  person all-around that the full-of-nonsense bull pricks me with anger-releasing emotions and frustrated hate. The generosity of the attention given to this heroine who I loathe blocks me from being able to force myself to read the story from beginning to end. I have tried SEVERAL TIMES. I have been inhibited SEVERAL TIMES. All of those times. Consistently and seemingly neverending-ly, all the characters angered me. Them standing up for this person whom is, in my point of view, mistakenly defended for (their righteousness needs to be corrected) and poorly judging a sane and correctly angered victim just.. <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1390110134ra/8145481.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> makes me unfathomably livid and loathe when I do not wish to. My hateful sentiments were stirred and boiled up and didn't die. <br><br>I may have<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/412290.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>And because my hate grew incessantly, needling me with its whiny heat, I started to hate the series since the characters I liked/loved became unmentionable beeps. It's safe and true to say I was livid with everyone. After some steam died off I read some of the books in the series again and her other series because I refused to believe this book ruined all others and I've come to the conclusion that No, it did not. I am still really fond of her series. This book was a damper though. It just tanked me up with spiteful and hurt-wanting feelings.<br><br>I pretty much threw all away for Thanatos. Peer Pressure and bullying. That's what happened. Thanatos was forced to like this Aegis trollop. By his friends and family and the author. Can there not be a logical no 'happily ever after' with the chosen heroine? PLEASE? They are not good for one another. They do not complement. And she only weakens and hurts him. She's like a parasite. She gains. All this love and acceptance and righteousness and he gets nothing. He tolerates and from peer pressure and bullying he accepts. She endangered the whole world and he gets the blame and bitching from others? What is wrong with people? The heroine is made out to be so good when she is so wrong and not good. Sure I get her mentality: When people believe something very strongly they become very scary in that they are fueled to do actions that result in objectionable consequences. Kind of like how some religions are so against each other they go into war or a country and another country deem themselves superior and go to war to prove their might, or Whites believe themselves more worthy than Blacks or any other color out there in this humongously multiracial world and create hurt and pain. Or me in my biased and hate-biting review. Consequences. Think of your damn consequences. That's why I edited this review to be less of a hateful person in my eyes and others. It seemed like Thanatos just went with the flow and author-manipulated lust to "go with the flow" and make the heroine his heroine. She raped him and took his first. I wonder if the bullying, peer pressure, uncertainty, lust, and his loss of innocence fueled him to make the tragedy of a decision to keep her as his forever-partner. I really think he needs to think more on the decision before jumping the gun. Divorce isn't doable and he's going to live on in tolerance if he takes this step. Which he idiotically does. I'm upset at the course of the events and the ending. And him. Plus everyone else.<br><br><br>I am not okay with this coupling. I join the small(?) number of people who despise the heroine. To me she is<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389606433ra/8043490.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>who happens to have one hell of a luckyarse luck and happened to land someone as amazing and caring as Thanatos. He's not perfect. But he's better than her.<br><br><br>--<br><br><br><br>A note I found in my Kindle readings:<br><br>"Balls: They've got balls. I wanna rip them off. She got hurt by her own fault and they blame him? She ran away. She raped him (drugs or not she would have and that is so 'convenient' for her to have been drugged too. Yes, now she has an EXCUSE for being a beep and getting away with anything and everything. This book is unbelievable. How they keep coming up with excuses for her and how all the beeps and beeps who should know themselves before talking to Thanatos like that go about licking her feet. And how...[unmentionables].."<br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="4360861195638435347" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/183416088?book_show_action=true">Jul 09, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aly is so frigging bored" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aly is so frigging bored" href="/user/show/4290492-aly-is-so-frigging-bored">Aly is so frigging bored</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Mass Market Paperback 9780446574501" href="/book/show/13057150-lethal-rider">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4290492-aly-is-so-frigging-bored?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer183416088&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer183416088" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9377730106916158438">WARNING: Author of this review will be a total fan-girl!<br/><br/>That being said I just love Larissa Ione! I love the way she writes, the characters she creates, the plots she develops, the settings she imagines, I just love everything she types[full-stop].<br/><br/>Thanatos is a little bit, let's say... miffed that he was tricked into having sex and he kind of let loose in the end of the last book. Now we fast forward 8 months and he finds out he's a dad. You can understand why he'll be shocked and more then piss</span>
  <span id="freeText9377730106916158438" style="display:none">WARNING: Author of this review will be a total fan-girl!<br /><br />That being said I just love Larissa Ione! I love the way she writes, the characters she creates, the plots she develops, the settings she imagines, I just love everything she types[full-stop].<br /><br />Thanatos is a little bit, let's say... miffed that he was tricked into having sex and he kind of let loose in the end of the last book. Now we fast forward 8 months and he finds out he's a dad. You can understand why he'll be shocked and more then pissed about being kept in the dark by everyone. Regan isn't having a better time of this either: she is scared for her child, she's swamped by remorse and, to add it all up, she feels she can't be a good mother or protect her child so she decided to give him up for adoption. <br /><br />That above is the setting on this novel and you can all understand why it'll be so epic, not that stopping the Apocalypse isn't a big enough battle. I loved how LI handled the emotions of every character in this book, we have fear for your child, love, the feeling of betrayal, self doubt...We have it all. <br /><br />This is by far the best she ever written, not that I don't feel this way with her every new book. Now I can't decide if I should torture myself by reading the first chapter in Resph's book or if I should wait a little for it :))<br /><br /><br />Quotes(it think some of them are a little spoilerish :D):<br />She raised her makeshift stake. “Get out of my way.”<br />He laughed. “Stupid, fat human. You’re no match for me.”<br />“Fat? Fat? I’m pregnant, you walking corpse. I might be fat, but you’re dead.”<br />.....................<br />“So did you get anything else?”<br />“Not a lot. But I can tell you that the kid is big. You’ve easily got a nine-pounder in there. He’s ripping some sort of powerful ability, and he’s obviously picky about who he lets touch his mom.” Shade looked over at Thanatos. “Or not picky.”<br />Thanatos arched a blond eyebrow. “That’s not very professional.”<br />Shade gave Than a droll stare. “I’m a demon. You want professional, haul her over to the Mayo Clinic.”<br />.........................<br />“There’s nothing wrong with the baby or Than or anything. It’s just…” Limos looked down at her bright green nails, which poked out of her fingerless gauntlets.<br />“It’s just what?”<br />Limos shifted her weight and looked at her other hand. “Shiny.”<br />“Limos!”<br />“Fine.”<br />.........................................<br />Wraith sauntered over to her, his blonde vampire mate, Serena, on his arm. “Congratulations, Aegi. If you need any tips on raising a kid, I’m there for you.”<br />“That’s sweet of you.” Serena patted his hand in that universal, yes-dear-I’ll-humor-you way. “But I’m sure Thanatos can mess up a kid as well as you can.”<br />“I doubt that.” Wraith planted a kiss on Serena’s neck, breaking it off when Thanatos punched him in the shoulder.</span>
  <a data-text-id="9377730106916158438" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

		    <b>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('vW0czPrqgdE+600L9qUbNGQ6oL3h+9CaaCH4apSpa2NiklQIVwh9vAKFGy7ASDb75GpjecxviU5ZOH+kYcArOA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('v9CYJ61iyqY7kB9HmtZ4ei0TbWIgCFHAzmvYfSK9bTRgL9DjAIA2ywf+SWKsO1W1rUOupg2cCBT/cl+z19Qtbw==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer3215750509415367320">Air Force veteran Larissa Ione traded in a career in meteorology to pursue her passion of writing. She has since published dozens of books, hit several bestseller lists, including the New York Times and USA Today, and has been nominated for a RITA award. She now spends her days in pajamas with her computer, strong coffee, and supernatural worlds. She believes in celebrating everything, and would n</span>
  <span id="freeText3215750509415367320" style="display:none">Air Force veteran Larissa Ione traded in a career in meteorology to pursue her passion of writing. She has since published dozens of books, hit several bestseller lists, including the New York Times and USA Today, and has been nominated for a RITA award. She now spends her days in pajamas with her computer, strong coffee, and supernatural worlds. She believes in celebrating everything, and would never be caught without a bottle of Champagne chilling in the fridge…just in case. She currently lives in Wisconsin with her retired U.S. Coast Guard husband, her son, a rescue cat named Vegas, and her very own hellhounds, a King Shepherd named Hexe and a Belgian Malinois named Duvel.</span>

Caught in a tug of war between Heaven and Hell, he must weigh his thirst for revenge against his desire for a mysterious female named Blaspheme—a female whose very origins could deliver him into salvation . . . or destruction.\n\nLIKE AN ANGEL SCORNED\n\nBlaspheme has a deadly secret: she\'s the forbidden offspring of an angel and a fallen angel. Hunted by both heavenly and satanic forces, she has survived only by laying low and trusting no one. When Revenant claims he can save them both, how can she possibly believe him? This partial loads on almost every page view.  The associated React component makes
a call to SignInPromptController#get to determine if the user should see the sign in interstial.
This is determined by how many signed out pagehits the user has executed an how recently they have
last seen the insterstitial.  If the controller responds indicating the popup should appear, the
